<review>I'm not sure where these negative reviews are coming from. I had put off checking out this shop, even though it's a couple blocks from my house, because of the bad reviews. I finally stopped by, figuring I'd at least see what it's like and they surely would have the couple basics I needed at the time. After staying far longer than I'd planned, and spending quite a bit more than I intended, I've gotta say that this is easily one of the best shops in town. Their selection is larger and more complete than a lot of the shops around here, and included things I'd been looking for for a while. Great selection of premium e-liquid, mods (authentic and clones, so there's something for any budget), RDAs, tanks, accessories... It's all there. The guys behind the counter when I was there were awesome. All in all, I'm looking forward to going back. This is a very nice place to have some fun! And it's open all year around! They have separate places for freestyle skating and tryouts/practices.
Shoes are in great condition, but not very comfortable, but they are rentals, so you can't expect more. If you want comfort- buy your own skates.
Locker system is a great idea, but be prepared, they accept only ¬¢25+¬¢25. Cafe accepts only cash. But they have ATM ready for you.

The rink is separated for the begginers and better skaters... They also have some buckets to lean on if you can't skate at all.
They also have supervises there if you need help.
It was a great experience. Will be going there soon again.</text>

The drinks take forever and most of the time they are made wrong. I have never written a review before but the customer service and work ethic here is so incredibly poor that I feel I have to say something. Every time that I order any food that has to be heated, they screw it up. For example, I ordered a bagel one time and when I actually got the bagel, it looked like they had just torn it apart. Another time, I ordered a breakfast sandwich and when I went to take it out of the bag, it was all taken apart and looked like they had just thrown it into the oven without any care at all. Everybody who works there always seems like they are high as a kite and just offer terrible costumer service. The only polite one there is Lupe and she usually works the cash register. I do not recommend this place at all. <user_name>Christopher Giuffre<//user_name><Date>1558654587790<//Date><Rating>5< /Rating>< Text>
The best Starbucks I've visited, no question! I'm so surprised there are low ratings at this location, but I do believe it's due to the San Francisco fast-paced way of life, and this location often being busy (and then drinks taking long).

But the staff at this Starbucks is so incredibly wonderful and personable, that you feel welcomed each time you visit. In the very busy FiDi, it's sometimes difficult to connect and find baristas who work to put a smile on your face. These people do just that, while working hard to stay up with orders. I have visited over 30 times, and each time I left feeling more energized and happier than when I came in. When it's busy, it may take longer, but this place, and the people working, remind me what matters most and that it's okay to slow down. Prepare to leave with a smile. Thank you all!</Text>

< Review>
Great place to get your car washed. Prices start at 6.00 and I believe go up to 14.00. I may be wrong. Anywho, the higher the prices the better your car is washed. Duh. I went and got the 6.00 car wash. While waiting for my car to be washed I noticed cars were coming out wet. I realized I would need something to dry it so I bought a microfiber towel. They're 2.00 and after you're done you can exchange it for a new one, pretty cool! After my car was washed, it was super wet so I gave it a quick dry. Regardless of it being wet, it was cleaned well. I was satisfied with the wash. I total I paid 8.00 for a good wash and a good vacuum. Will return, the only reason I gave it 4 stars is because of the wet car.< /Review>
